## Text Elements
Graph Laplacian Learning to infer 
class labels for unlabeled pixels ^OanIctVF

Given q end-members, acquire a 
one-hot pseudo-label vector q*
to identify the most significant 
end member of this node (pixel) ^dnC8qKBB

training pixels
(labeled pixel) ^BMHB914P

to compute their respective values ^abi29tqr

Sequential Active Learning or LocalMax: ^zHv1kxUa

Add a query set of unlabeled pixels
to the current training pixel set
based on the acquisition values ^ZlU0oHWJ

q* ^aGGm3XWL

q* ^i7iTY9wF

Repeat until the desired number of 
training pixels is reached ^uwGBTidt

q* =  ^VwVcKO17

q* =  ^BMxNWyka

q* =  ^7eFnLtNq

One-hot pseudo-labeling vector (i.e., ground truth) for training pixels ^qcbDTlHc

q* ^x7oT2JTc

Terminate the loop until a number of 
M desired training pixels is reached
(Assume that M = 3 in our example) ^dspDwMJ6

q* =  ^eTKfeaSE

an example output vector for each node after Graph Laplacian Learning ^XpRxXKxJ

q* ^NNUX7r1B

q ^cTiwI0rD

q ^gAA9yjkk

q ^RlxIc8Zw

q ^C4DdSuQ4

q ^vJIuFFjt

q ^A3EGmCvF

q ^iXfdZgZ8

where q is a vector whose entries are probabilities over all given classes. 
Each entry is nonnegative and all entries sum up to 1 ^GGFoslaG

For each output vector, infer the index of the entry with the highest probability value.
The index corresponds to a specific label (or class)  ^ljgoKzuA

all entries are non-negative and 
sum up to 1 ^MCyE7ZXm

the K-th entry is the highest value,
so the K-end member is the class for this vector, 
and the one-hot pseudo-labeling is q ^5pSb3Ggm

Graph-based Active Learning to Pick Training Pixels ^suzufP3T

q* ^F1y1snYH

q* ^d9FeW4Kd

duplicate nodes ^68FwMbYX

q* ^RiPFLXpr

Construct another graph and compute the new Laplacian matrix ^GnWmz8nR

Suppose that originally we have a data matrix A of dimension q x N,
and a training data matrix q x M A^, we concatenate them and have
a new data matrix (M + N) x (M + N) A*
 ^LvAy08bI

Break the Laplacian matrix into block form ^i7dUeEEl

A_GLU is an abundance map where each column is the abundance vector of each pixel in the hyperspectral imaging ^71ByNvfJ

solved via a closed-form solution ^FIhJ4ILP

= max(0, S^0_GLU) ^xxjuXseH

Replace any negative entries with 0 effectively ^OIVbsvQe
